 Of course, the communal powers continued to play their open game in both the places and so many people were also forced to leave their respective countries who did not approve of such division
 itihaas kii yah bhishantam traasadee isliye lagaataar badi hoti gai ki is desh main lagaataar ve sanghathan majboot hote gaye jinhone dharmik bhedbhaav or sampradayik tanaav ko badhaava diya
 Post-independence India was not as sensitive as it should have been on the right to civil equality - this is a big truth and many Congress governments will have to be held responsible for this
 yah bhi duhraana hoga ki bharat ne aazaadee kii ladaai ke dauraan apana jo anoothaa samaveshi rashtrawaad viksit kiya or jiske tahat ek samaveshi swapn vaala samvidhan banaaya, usko majboot karne kaa kaam jis tarah hona chahie tha, us tarah congress ne nahin kiya
 But the powers that want to create a new India today are betraying a greater legacy of freedom
 ve hindustan ke ek hazaar saal ke itihaas ko mitaa kar use uske peeche le janaa chaahati hai
 This is not possible scientifically nor historically
 isliye yah koshish aisa kataa-chanta vikrut manovigyaan bana rahi he jisamen baat to samanvay kii ho rahi he, lekin kaam vaimnasy bharaa ho rahaa he
 The citizenship amendment bill is also part of this mindset
 padosi deshon main sataae ja rahe alpsankhyakon ke naam par vah desh ke bahut bade samudaay ke bheetar yah ehsaas bharaa ja rahaa he ki unhen pehle darje kaa naagarik nahin mana ja rahaa
 Of course, despite the country's own traditions and all kinds of chaos and feudal trends after independence, its democratic temperament, which is slowly evolving, compels the ideology to show full generosity, at least at the level of statements
 lekin zyaada bady sachai yah he ki yah udaar parampara philhal harati lag rahi he or iske nattejey is desh ke liye kaase nuqasaandeh honge
 Of course, this country will prove to be much stronger than such forces, but by then many scratches that have been on the mind and heart will take time to overcome
 oxford shabdkosh (oxford Dictionary) ne shanivaar ko 'narishakthi' ko varsh 2018 ke liye hindi verde of da year (saal kaa hindi shabd) ghoshit kiya
 This announcement was made at the Jaipur Literature Festival
 oxford shabdkosh ne ek bayaan main kaha ki 'hindi verde of da year' kaa darja aise shabd ko diya jaataa he, jisaki ore se puure saal kaaphi dhyaan aakarshith karata he or lokachar, bhav or chintaa ko pratibimbit karata he
 The word 'nari' derived from Sanskrit means woman and Shakti means strength
 oxford shabdkosh kii ore se kaha gaya ki aaj yah shabd apni jindagi kaa bhaar uthaane vaali mahilaon kaa suchak he
 Nari Shakti was voted Hindi Word of the Year in India by the Oxford Dictionary with the help of an advisory committee of language experts
 is samiti main ashok kumaar sharma, kritika agarwal or namita gokhale va anya shaamil the
